### 1. 皮克斯风格微缩互动肖像

**Author**: [Taaruk](https://x.com/Taaruk_)  **Date**: 2026-01-11  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于创建一幅影棚肖像。该肖像将逼真的人类主体与一个迷你的、皮克斯风格的 3D 卡通版人物无缝融合，重点是人类手中握着小卡通人物的玩乐互动场景，采用柔和的电影级灯光和深蓝色渐变背景。

![皮克斯风格微缩互动肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768225992625_s3z1r9_G-XpUxnaEAAITff.jpg)
![皮克斯风格微缩互动肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768225993072_pmtj99_G-XpUyoasAIvEGh.jpg)

```
{
  "Objective": "Create a studio portrait blending a real human with a tiny Pixar-style 3D cartoon version of themselves in a playful, whimsical interaction",
  "PersonaDetails": {
    "PrimarySubject": {
      "Type": "Real human",
      "Wardrobe": "Casual {argument name="clothing color" default="grey"} sweater or t-shirt",
      "Expression": "Surprised and delighted",
      "Pose": "Holding a tiny character in one hand and pointing at it with the other",
      "Skin": "Photorealistic skin texture with natural detail"
    },
    "SecondarySubject": {
      "Type": "Tiny 3D cartoon version of the human",
      "Scale": "Miniature, resting in the human’s hand",
      "Style": "Pixar-style 3D character",
      "Proportions": "Exaggerated cute proportions with rounded features",
      "FacialFeatures": {
        "Eyes": "Large, expressive",
        "Expression": "Friendly, playful"
      },
      "Consistency": "Matching hairstyle and outfit of the real human"
    }
  },
  "Composition": {
    "Framing": "Medium close-up studio portrait",
    "InteractionFocus": "Clear visual relationship between human and miniature character",
    "DepthOfField": "Shallow depth of field",
    "Focus": "Ultra-sharp focus on both faces"
  },
  "LightingAndBackground": {
    "LightingStyle": "Soft cinematic studio lighting",
    "LightQuality": "Smooth highlights with gentle shadow falloff",
    "Background": "Dark blue gradient studio backdrop",
    "Separation": "Subtle rim light for subject-background separation"
  },
  "ArtDirection": {
    "StyleFusion": [
      "Photorealistic human portrait photography",
      "High-quality Pixar-style 3D character rendering"
    ],
    "Integration": "Seamless blending between real and 3D elements",
    "DetailLevel": "Ultra-detailed textures on skin, fabric, and 3D materials"
  },
  "MoodAndTone": {
    "Mood": "Whimsical, fun, lighthearted",
    "Energy": "Playful surprise and delight"
  },
  "PhotographyStyle": {
    "Genre": "Professional studio portrait photography",
    "CameraLook": "High-end cinematic realism",
    "ImageQuality": "High resolution, clean and sharp"
  },
  "NegativePrompt": [
    "uncanny valley",
    "cartoon human",
    "low-quality 3D",

```
Ultra-realistic, photorealistic studio portrait of an extremely beautiful young adult woman (18–20 years old). She has long, straight {argument name="hair color" default="blonde"} hair with a natural silky texture, delicately framing her face. Facial features are soft and refined with a balanced, feminine bone structure; small straight nose; smooth jawline; and subtle cheek definition. Large, sparkling light-blue eyes with realistic catchlights, long natural lashes, and softly defined brows. Perfect clear skin with natural pores and lifelike texture, soft peach undertones, no blemishes. Minimal, natural makeup: light foundation, gentle blush, soft nude lips, faint eye makeup enhancing realism. Gentle, dreamy expression with relaxed eyes and slightly parted lips.
She is wearing a black ribbed deep V-neck cropped tank top, paired with an oversized white button-up shirt worn open and loosely slipping off her shoulders. High-waisted light blue jeans with a modern casual fit. Trendy, effortless fashion styling. Standing pose, relaxed posture, one hand raised into her hair in a natural candid gesture.
Soft, diffused natural studio lighting that flatters the face, subtle highlights on hair and skin, smooth shadows, no harsh contrast. Neutral gray studio background with slight gradient for depth. Sharp focus on the face, shallow depth of field.       }

      "head_angle": "straight",

### 20. 杂乱室内一位东亚女性的电影肖像

**Author**: [路飞 🏴‍☠️ AI 研究员🧐](https://x.com/0xluffy_eth)  **Date**: 2026-01-08  **Language**: zh

> 一个高度详细的 Nano Banana Pro 提示词，用于生成一张电影感十足、氛围浓厚的年轻东亚女性肖像。该提示词细致地定义了拍摄对象的姿势、表情、服装、光线（黄金时段的强烈逆光）、环境（杂乱的室内）和相机设置（浅景深、胶片感），以实现一种梦幻、怀旧的美学，让人联想到日本摄影集。

![杂乱室内一位东亚女性的电影肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967482547_h5ufqb_G-HOY0wa0AAA-tl.jpg)

```
主体：年轻东亚女性，侧身回望镜头。肩膀看向后方，头部微微倾斜，身体背向摄像机。

表情：柔和、中性至略带忧郁，沉思凝视，嘴唇微启。

服装：深色结构化夹克或西装，可能是细条纹或纹理面料。大部分被阴影和前景元素遮挡。

头发：深棕色至黑色。长波浪卷，蓬松纹理。强烈逆光，在散落发丝上形成光晕效果。

面部：肤色偏白/苍白，暖色调。柔和脸型，杏眼，自然眉毛。最少化妆，裸妆风格。

环境：杂乱室内空间，似工作室、储藏室或老旧书店。木质架子堆满模糊物品、纸张、盒子和塑料包装。

前景：模糊透明物体（玻璃、塑料片、防尘套）形成多层反射。

光源：左侧窗户射入自然光。金色时刻，温暖扩散光。强逆光、体积灯光、镜头光晕、柔和眩光、明暗对比。

摄影机：眼平视角，透过前景遮挡物拍摄。浅景深（散焦），眼睛/脸部清晰，背景前景模糊。软焦、胶片颗粒、轻微晕影。

风格：电影感、氛围、怀旧、日常片段、飘飘然。

心情：梦幻、亲密、宁静、伤感。

参考：电影摄影、日本相册风格。
```

[[Shallow Depth Of Field]] [[Film Grain Aesthetic]] [[Nostalgic Mood]]

### 21. K-Pop 偶像肖像网格，用于快速选择

**Author**: [クロガネ@即覚醒させる人](https://x.com/mak0chipdf)  **Date**: 2026-01-08  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细 JSON 结构化提示，旨在根据输入照片快速生成九种 K-Pop 偶像肖像变体。该提示指定了拍摄对象的人口统计学特征、时尚、姿势、夜间公园环境以及技术相机设置（3:4 宽高比、暖色街灯、浅景深），以营造“男友感”美学。输出以 3x3 网格排列，并带有编号选项，以便快速选择和高分辨率输出所选图像。

![K-Pop 偶像肖像网格，用于快速选择](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967491658_7q0jgb_G-HDTzca0AcVzq9.jpg)
![K-Pop 偶像肖像网格，用于快速选择](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967492144_ipaajs_G-HDUTma0AANv1A.jpg)

```
この人物の顔のみに使用して下記のプロンプトへ適用させてください
実際のモデル撮影のように表情を変えながら9種類の異なるアングルで3×3のグリッドレイアウトで配置。各画像の左上に通し番号を1から順に表示して
{
  "subject_details": {
    "demographics": "Young Asian male, approx 20-25 years old, handsome K-pop idol aesthetic",
    "hair": "Black hair, medium length, curtain bangs / comma hairstyle, soft and natural texture",
    "face": "Looking directly at the camera (eye contact), calm and gentle expression, clear skin",
    "accessories": "Small silver earring in left ear"
  },
  "fashion": {
    "top": "Oversized black knitted crewneck sweater, visible ribbed texture",
    "bottom": "Grey pleated dress trousers / slacks",
    "waist": "Black leather belt with simple buckle"
  },
  "pose_and_action": {
    "posture": "Sitting relaxed on a wooden park bench, body facing slightly forward",
    "hand_action": "Right hand holding black thick-rimmed glasses (removed from face), held at chest level",
    "gaze": "Direct intense eye contact with the viewer",
    "other_hand": "Left hand resting on thigh"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "Public park at night",
    "season": "Late autumn / Fall",
    "ground": "Covered with brown fallen dry leaves",
    "background": "Dark trees, distant blurred city lights (bokeh), abstract sculpture silhouette",
    "nearby_objects": "Black backpack resting on the bench next to the subject"
  },
  "technical_specs": {
    "lighting": "Warm artificial street lighting from the side, creating soft shadows on face",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4 (vertical portrait)",
    "camera_style": "Portrait photography, medium long shot, framing the subject from about 2-3 meters away, sharp focus on subject, shallow depth of field",
    "mood": "Romantic, intimate, boyfriend material (Namchin-jal), night date vibe",
    "color_palette": "Black, warm orange/brown, dark grey"
  }
}
```

### 31. 电影感复古室内人像，基于照片参考

**Author**: [Raylan](https://x.com/Raylan89)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: en

> 一个提示，指示 Nano Banana Pro 将上传的照片转换为电影感、情绪化的室内肖像，同时保持拍摄对象的精确特征和服装形状，并将其置于一个带有暖钨灯照明和浅景深的复古客厅中。

![电影感复古室内人像，基于照片参考](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804055417_210kqd_G989CH6bcAMkepB.jpg)
![电影感复古室内人像，基于照片参考](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804055750_73wqp6_G989CH-asAAfu5_.jpg)

```
using my photo as the main reference, create a cinematic, moody indoor portrait. keep my exact facial features, hairstyle, skin tone, and outfit shape. place me sitting on a wooden stool in a vintage living-room with warm tungsten lighting. add soft shadows and a cozy, retro atmosphere. behind me, include wooden wall panels, old stereo speakers, vinyl records, and a low shelf with ceramic vases. maintain a shallow depth of field with soft blur in the background.

keep the colors warm—browns, ambers, and orange highlights. the style should be cinematic, soft, and film-like, with natural skin texture, realistic lighting, and a quiet, contemplative mood. full-body shot, slightly low angle, 35mm lens look
```

### 54. Nano Banana Pro 的折纸风格转换提示

**Author**: [ハヤテ](https://x.com/hayate1ex)  **Date**: 2025-12-31  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个用于 Nano Banana Pro（与 Gemini 搭配使用）的提示，旨在将现有插图转换为折纸风格的图像。它指定使用千代纸、浅景深和对角俯视视角，同时保持原始插图的宽高比和高分辨率。

![Nano Banana Pro 的折纸风格转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767456265114_i2hlg4_G9eB5LQa4AE5zaR.jpg)

```
# テイスト・照明・アングル
追加したイラスト参照。
アスペクト比1:1、4K解像度、非常に詳細、
超リアル、広角レンズ、偏光フィルター、HDR。

# 折り紙
追加したイラストを千代紙で折られた折り紙風で描く。
被写界深度は浅く、正面から見た斜め俯瞰図。
```

![高山背景下的高端冬季产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454966661_n2ojtb_G9bOQxDaYAA6Z2v.jpg)
![高山背景下的高端冬季产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454967396_lbw9gu_G9bOQxfbAAALGdV.jpg)
![高山背景下的高端冬季产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454967882_rnp7z6_G9bOQzGbkAE9jnc.jpg)
![高山背景下的高端冬季产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454969142_c826ow_G9bOQz5aYAAjgG4.jpg)

```
A single, high-quality product item positioned centrally in the snow.
(Note for generation:

Insert specific object here, e.g., "{argument name="product example 1" default="A white ceramic teapot with gold trim and 'WINTERBREW' logo"}," "{argument name="product example 2" default="A clear glass perfume bottle with silver cap and 'ALPINE ESSENCE' text"}," or "{argument name="product example 3" default="A pair of brown leather hiking boots covered in light snow"}.")
accessories
Natural, thematic elements scattered artfully on the immediate snow surface surrounding the main subject. Examples include pinecones, whole cinnamon sticks, star anise, frosted lavender sprigs, small pine branches, or complementary items like a knit beanie.
environment
A pristine, sunlit winter alpine landscape. The immediate foreground is deep, textured powder snow. The mid-ground features snow-laden evergreen trees. The background is dominated by majestic, rugged alpine mountain peaks under a clear or slightly hazy blue sky. A rustic wooden chalet or cabin is visible in the middle distance, slightly blurred.
lighting
Bright, crisp, natural daylight. Sunny conditions creating sparkling highlights on the snow crystals and the product surface, casting distinct, cool shadows.
camera
Professional commercial photography. High resolution, macro detail sharp focus on the main subject. Shallow depth of field (bokeh), creating a softly blurred background of the mountains and trees. Shot from a slightly low or eye-level angle relative to the product placed on the snow.
style
High-end product photography with a cozy, luxurious, fresh, and serene winter atmosphere. The composition is balanced and naturalistic.
```

### 58. 生活方式肖像摄影的详细 JSON 提示词

**Author**: [Heisenberg](https://x.com/rovvmut_)  **Date**: 2025-12-30  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示词，专为图像生成模型设计，详细说明了生活方式肖像照片的参数。它包括构图、主体细节（一位抱着狗的年轻女性）、环境、光照、调色板、技术相机设置和艺术风格，旨在营造一种温暖、坦率的都市美学，并具有浅景深效果。

```
{
"image_type": "photograph",
"orientation": "portrait",
"composition": {
"framing": "medium shot",
"camera_angle": "eye-level",
"subject_placement": "centered with slight left bias",
"depth_of_field": "shallow",
"background_blur": "strong bokeh",
"balance": "asymmetrical but visually balanced",
"crop": "above knees"
},
"subjects": [
{
"type": "human",
"gender_presentation": "{argument name="gender" default="female"}",
"age_range": "young adult",
"pose": "standing, holding dog close to torso",
"expression": "soft smile, relaxed",
"gaze": "toward camera",
"hair": {
"color": "dark grey",
"style": "short"
},
"clothing": {
"top": "white lightweight button-up shirt",
"inner_layer": "black sleeveless top",
"bottom": "blue denim jeans",
"style": "casual, urban"
}
},
{
"type": "animal",
"species": "dog",
"breed_appearance": "small poodle-type",
"fur": {
"color": "{argument name="dog color" default="reddish brown"}",
"texture": "curly, dense"
},
"pose": "cradled in arms, legs relaxed",
"accessories": "dark leash attached"
}
],
"environment": {
"setting": "{argument name="setting" default="outdoor urban park or pedestrian area"}",
"background_elements": [
"trees",
"paved walkway",
"distant buildings",
"blurred pedestrians"
],
"season_impression": "spring or mild summer"
},
"lighting": {
"type": "natural daylight",
"quality": "soft and diffused",
"direction": "frontal with slight overhead",
"shadows": "minimal and soft",
"highlights": "gentle skin highlights"
},
"color_palette": {
"dominant_colors": [
"white",
"soft green",
"warm brown",
"muted blue"
],
"tone": "warm-neutral",
"saturation": "moderate",
"contrast": "low to moderate"
},
"technical_details": {
"camera_type": "DSLR or mirrorless",
"lens_characteristics": "wide aperture portrait lens",
"approx_aperture": "f/1.8–f/2.8",
"focal_length_estimate": "50mm–85mm equivalent",
"sharpness": "high on subjects, soft background",
"noise": "minimal"
},
"artistic_style": {
"genre": "lifestyle portrait photography",
"mood": "warm, friendly, candid",
"aesthetic": "clean, modern, natural",
"post_processing": {
"skin_tones": "natural and even",
"color_grading": "light warm adjustment",
"retouching": "minimal"
}
},
"background": {

"function": "contextual without distraction",
"lighting_consistency": "matches subject lighting"
},

Shot on a professional camera, shallow depth of field, sharp focus on the subject’s face, background softly blurred. Editorial fashion portrait style, cinematic café photography, emotional, minimal, and artistic mood.
Color style: pure monochrome black and white, no color, no tint, no warm or cool tones.
Aspect ratio: portrait orientation, magazine style framing.
Ultra-high resolution, ultra-realistic skin texture, natural imperfections visible, no over-smoothing, no artificial look.

The background is a completely blurred, dreamy wash of snowy pines and a pale grey sky, with no structural elements visible. The composition is dominated by the woman's upper body and the soft foreground elements.

### 82. 图书馆里一位男士的电影时尚大片

> 这是一个为 Gemini 应用设计的图像生成提示，旨在制作电影般的时尚大片。场景设定在一个尘土飞扬的图书馆中，一位男士身穿量身定制的米色大衣，强调一种情绪化、氛围感的画面，采用温暖的大地色调和浅景深。提示中包含了详细的相机技术规格，如镜头、光圈、ISO 和宽高比，以实现高质量、专业的视觉效果。

### 110. 室内人像精修，景深虚化效果

**Author**: [Iqra Saifi](https://x.com/IqraSaifiii)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张年轻亚洲女性的逼真、精致肖像，她戴着眼镜，坐在一张皮扶手椅上。该提示详细说明了她的服装（细条纹衬衫裙、过膝袜）、姿势（眨眼，手靠近脸颊）以及精确的相机设置（35mm/50mm，f/2.0-f/2.8），以实现浅景深和温暖的室内照明。

![室内人像精修，景深虚化效果](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237877154_k547uv_G8eHqWubcAAzZe_.jpg)

```
Subject: A photorealistic portrait of a young Asian woman with voluminous, long, wavy black hair and fair skin. She is wearing thin-rimmed, round glasses and has a playful expression, winking one eye with a subtle smile.
Outfit: She is dressed in a black, long-sleeved button-down shirt dress with thin white vertical pinstripes. She is wearing sheer black thigh-high stockings.
Pose: She is seated in a curved, cream-colored leather armchair. Her body is angled slightly forward. Her right hand is raised, with long manicured fingers delicately touching her cheek and jawline in a playful, posing gesture.
Environment: The background features soft, floor-length beige or off-white sheer curtains, suggesting an indoor hotel room or bedroom setting at night.
Lighting & Style: Warm, soft indoor lighting that creates gentle highlights on her hair and the silky texture of the shirt. High-resolution photography, sharp focus on the face, slightly candid but polished aesthetic.
Camera Angle: Slightly high angle (tilted down about 10–15 degrees), seated eye-level.
Focal Length: 35mm or 50mm. (This creates a natural perspective without too much distortion, typical of high-end smartphone portraits or standard portrait lenses).
Aperture: f/2.0 to f/2.8. (This provides a shallow depth of field, keeping her face and hand in sharp focus while softly blurring the texture of the curtains in the background).
Shutter Speed: 1/60s or 1/100s. (Standard for indoor handheld shots to avoid motion blur).
ISO: 400 to 800. (Slightly higher sensitivity to account for the warm, dim indoor lighting without introducing too much grain).
Lighting Setup: Soft key light from the front-top (likely a ceiling fixture or ring light), creating the specular highlights on the nose and forehead.
```

### 112. 立体模型重新诠释提示词

**Author**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 给 Nano Banana Pro 的一个提示，指示模型使用上传的图像作为参考，并将场景重新诠释为一个人手中拿着的小型、逼真、高质量的立体模型，强调微距摄影、浅景深和超精细纹理。

![立体模型重新诠释提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237897029_q5xb0q_G8dUElkXQAA_il_.jpg)

```

      "film_grain": "very light to preserve photorealism"
    },
    "creative_notes": "keep colors natural-looking despite vivid blue; preserve fine fibrous texture and droplet realism; avoid artificial gradients",
    "signature": "VIVEK HY"
  }
}
```

### 147. 逼真的编辑肖像模板（JSON 格式）

**Author**: [AltSociety AI](https://x.com/AltSocietyAI)  **Date**: 2025-12-08  **Language**: en

> 一个可复用的 JSON 提示模板，用于生成高度逼真、精致且具有编辑级品质的肖像。它详细指定了相机设置（定焦镜头、浅景深）、光照、美学氛围以及逼真皮肤和头发细节等主体特征。

![逼真的编辑肖像模板（JSON 格式）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438542637_1skf1v_G7pUQSiboAAYIOA.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": {
    "scene": "{{Describe the scene + subject here}}",

    "style": {
      "camera": {
        "shot_type": "portrait, medium-full or full body",
        "lens": "50mm/85mm prime lens shallow depth of field",
        "aperture": "f/1.4 – f/2.8",
        "lighting": "soft directional studio lighting or natural warm light",
        "focus": "sharp on face + eyes, gentle background falloff"
      },

      "environment": {
        "background": "minimal, clean interior or subtle natural background",
        "colors": "neutral tones, soft whites, blacks, muted warm palette",
        "texture": "smooth skin, natural grain, cinematic contrast"
      },

      "aesthetic": {
        "mood": "confident, relaxed, elegant",
        "tone": "modern beauty photography, fashion editorial energy",
        "emotion": "soft pose, natural expression, well-framed composition"
      },

      "subject_features": {
        "skin_detail": "realistic pores, natural highlights, subtle blush",
        "hair": "defined strands, smooth natural flow",
        "makeup": "soft glam, clean shading, prominent eye definition"
      },

      "clothing_styling": {
        "fit": "form-fitting modern outfit or fashion-forward styling",
        "material_detail": "accurate fabric sheen + texture rendering",
        "accessories": "minimal jewelry, elegant accents if needed"
      },

      "render_quality": {
        "resolution": "8k ultra fine detail",
        "post_process": "cinematic color grade, smooth noise, high clarity",
        "realism": "photo-realistic but polished, editorial quality"
      }
    }
  }
}
```

### 157. 黄金时段豪华跑车人像提示，带面部锁定

**Author**: [Javeriya Editor](https://x.com/JadoonKhan281)  **Date**: 2025-12-07  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计的极其详细的提示，专注于在黄金时段的豪华跑车内生成一张超逼真的 8K RAW 照片。该提示严格要求将女性和男性的面部、头发和衣服锁定到提供的参考图像。它指定了胶片模拟（Portra 400）、浅景深（f/1.4）、微观细节（皮肤毛孔、灰尘颗粒）和光线（柔和漫射的阳光），以实现高对比度、抓拍式且时尚的美学效果。

![黄金时段豪华跑车人像提示，带面部锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421956363_yce03x_G7iZYgya4AAbc-M.jpg)

```
Edit the image, ensuring the face, hair, and clothes for BOTH the woman and the man are kept 100% identical to their respective uploaded images. These elements are locked and must not be changed or edited in any way. **Subjects** * **The Woman**: As described below, with face, hair, and clothes from her uploaded image. * **The Man**: He is the driver. His face, hair, and clothes should be kept 100% identical to a reference image. He has a relaxed and calm demeanor that complements the woman's style. **Realism & Photographic Details** * **Photography Style**: Ultra-realistic, photorealistic, 8K, RAW photo. * **Camera & Lens**: Shot on a 35mm film camera with a 50mm f/1.4 lens. Introduce subtle lens distortion and very slight chromatic aberration on the edges of high-contrast areas. * **Film & Grain**: Emulate the look of Portra 400 film with fine, natural film grain. Add halation, a soft red glow around highlights. * **Focus & Sharpeness**: Use a shallow depth of field (f/1.4) to create a soft, blurry background (bokeh). The focus should be critically sharp on the woman's eyes, with a natural fall-off. The man will be slightly less in focus. The overall image should not be artificially sharpened. * **Texture & Micro-details**: Render hyper-realistic skin texture on the woman, including visible pores, fine lines, and nearly invisible vellus hair (peach fuzz). Fabric textures on the car interior should be highly detailed. Capture subtle imperfections like dust motes in the air, fingerprints on the car window, and minor reflections on the glossy lips. **Lighting & Mood** * **Source & Quality**: Natural, soft-diffused sunlight from the "golden hour" (late afternoon) streaming through the car's side window (passenger side). * **Effect**: The light should cast soft shadows and create a warm, gentle glow primarily on the right side of the woman's face. The man, in the driver's seat, will be more in shadow, creating depth and dimension in the scene. Create specular highlights on the woman's cheekbones and glossy lips. * **Contrast**: The car's interior should be in shadow, creating a high-contrast scene that makes the subjects pop. **Pose & Composition** * **Scene**: A candid, stylish moment inside a **luxury sports car, open roof type** featuring two people. * **Woman's Pose**: She is in the passenger seat, leaning forward slightly, resting her chin on one hand in a candid, thoughtful, or slightly bored manner. * **Man's Pose**: He is in the driver's seat, relaxed, with one hand resting on the steering wheel. He is looking forward, focused on the road, or taking a quick, natural glance toward the woman. * **Angle**: Shot from a slightly low angle from the passenger side. * **Framing**: The woman is the primary subject in the foreground. Include her knees/legs to enhance the candid, casual feel. The man is partially framed, visible from the chest up. **Woman's Details** * **Expression**: A neutral, calm, confide
```

      },

    },

    "photography": {

```
